- [2026-05-14] OUT01 outbox payload safety boundary **DONE** - resolved Q-051 for M1 with a 64 KiB UTF-8 JSON hard cap on outbox event payloads. `OutboxPayload.Create` rejects oversized serialized payloads before returning a `JsonDocument`, and `OutboxEvent.Create` validates direct `JsonDocument` payloads before persistence. Event payloads are not silently truncated; existing `last_error` truncation remains separate at 2,000 characters. While verifying that proof, OUT01 fixed a pre-existing circular RLS policy dependency between `assignment` and `invitation_token` that caused Postgres `42P17 infinite recursion` before the new assertion could run. ## Queue head after LS01 - 2026-05-17

LS01 is validated and Q-042 is closed for the M1 baseline. The next non-UX runtime slice is:

**LS02 - Launch packet downstream provenance consumers**

Goal: make report/export/proof surfaces consume the frozen launch packet where provenance is needed, rather than reconstructing launch context from mutable campaign setup state. Keep the scope backend/runtime only; do not start UX/UI work.

Acceptance direction:

- Report proof and export provenance can identify the launch packet schema version and frozen launch sections used for scoring/policy interpretation.
- Consumers continue to avoid raw answers, recipient/provider fields, salts, tokens, tenant IDs, and public item text.
- Existing scalar snapshot columns remain supported while downstream readers migrate to packet-aware provenance.
- Add regression coverage proving a post-launch setup mutation does not alter packet-derived provenance.

Report and wave proof responses now expose launch packet schema version and section names from the frozen launch snapshot; report-proof CSV/codebook exports include the same provenance. Docker-backed report/export/wave tests were selected but skipped locally, so CI or a Docker-enabled session should run them before treating LS02 as fully CI-validated.

## Done - 2026-05-18 D271/D272 full default staging release runner live proof
- D271 assessment selected live release-runner proof because D270 integrated backup/restore into the default live gate, but only the skipped-live path had been verified.
- D272 ran the full default `deploy/staging/run-release-checks.ps1` with no skip flags. The first run passed build/static/Node/web/Compose/local-smoke/product-spine steps, then exposed real backup/restore smoke bugs.
- Root causes fixed: PowerShell split the pg_dump shell command around `$backupFileName`; Docker stderr/progress was treated as terminating PowerShell errors before `$LASTEXITCODE` was checked; restore pg_restore needed the `platform_worker` role because restored RLS policy targets it; local `.env` omits `POSTGRES_WORKER_USER` while Compose defaults it to `platform_worker`; restore verification SQL was truncated through nested `sh -c` quoting.
- Fixes: `backup-restore-smoke.ps1` now builds pg_dump/pg_restore shell commands as single arguments, captures native stderr while checking exit codes explicitly, defaults the restore worker role to `platform_worker` unless env overrides it, bootstraps that role with `createuser`, and runs restore verification queries through direct `docker compose exec -e PGPASSWORD=... psql ... -c` arguments instead of nested shell SQL.
- Added static regression coverage in `StagingWorkerDeploymentPackageTests.Backup_restore_smoke_passes_container_commands_as_single_shell_arguments`.
- Verification: RED regression failed on missing command guards; direct backup/restore smoke passed with non-empty dump and 53 public tables / 52 public relations; full default release runner passed with build, 34/34 staging deployment package static tests, 24/24 Node deployment package tests, web audit/check/build, bundle budgets, local and VPS Compose config rendering, local staging smoke, product-spine smoke, and backup/restore smoke; final `dotnet build --no-restore` passed with 0 warnings and 0 errors.
- Remaining risk: This is local/default staging proof, not a remote VPS deployment rehearsal or production legal/GDPR/SLA readiness. D273 should reassess remote/VPS proof, withdrawal legal-operability evidence, report/PDF/export value, and in-app notification/admin workflow gaps while Q-054 blocks outbound operational-notification email.
